     <script type="text/javascript">
      var svgFlashLoad = {
				addSVGIcons : function() {
				var DccUserInfo = sessionStorage.getItem('dccUserCookie'),
					cartURLInfo = sessionStorage.getItem('cartURL'),
					displayCartFlag = sessionStorage.getItem('displayCartFlag');
					if(DccUserInfo) {
						var mainNav = document.querySelector('nav.mega__main');
						mainNav.classList.add('loggedInUser');
						if (displayCartFlag == 'true') {
							var cartOuterDiv = document.querySelector('.mega__cart.icon.button--cart');
							cartOuterDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
							var cartContent = document.querySelector('.mega__cart .mini-cart');
							cartContent.setAttribute('href', cartURLInfo);
						}
					}
					var languageDropdown = document.querySelector('.component-geolocationLanguage');
					languageDropdown.addEventListener("click", function(e){
						var element = document.querySelector(".component-geolocationLanguage .dropdown");
						element.classList.toggle("open");
					});
				}
			}
			svgFlashLoad.addSVGIcons();
     </script>
